<div id="review_526070901" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/526070901" />
    <a title="Jacqueline&#39;s Reads" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4197769-jacqueline-s-reads"><img alt="Jacqueline&#39;s Reads" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1380942477p2/4197769.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/526070901?book_show_action=true">Feb 04, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jacqueline&#39;s Reads" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jacqueline&#39;s Reads" href="/user/show/4197769-jacqueline-s-reads">Jacqueline&#39;s Reads</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4197769-jacqueline-s-reads?shelf=5-stars-favorites">5-stars-favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer526070901" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14527664230094004713"><b>5 Stars!!!</b><br/><br/><b>”You’re the sun I revolve around…”</b><br/><br/>From page 1… <b>I absolutely, jumping-for-joy LOVED</b> <i>THE UNWANTED WIFE</i>!!! <br/><br/>Theresa has been married to her cold husband, Alessandro, for over a year and half and finally she requested a divorced. Alessandro refuses to divorce her until he gets a son. Theresa doesn’t understand why Alessandro won’t divorce her and Teresa is tired of being the quiet “doormat” wife. As Theresa finally voices her opinion, Alessandro sees a different side of Theresa and doesn’t </span>
  <span id="freeText14527664230094004713" style="display:none"><b>5 Stars!!!</b><br><br><b>”You’re the sun I revolve around…”</b><br><br>From page 1… <b>I absolutely, jumping-for-joy LOVED</b> <i>THE UNWANTED WIFE</i>!!! <br><br>Theresa has been married to her cold husband, Alessandro, for over a year and half and finally she requested a divorced. Alessandro refuses to divorce her until he gets a son. Theresa doesn’t understand why Alessandro won’t divorce her and Teresa is tired of being the quiet “doormat” wife. As Theresa finally voices her opinion, Alessandro sees a different side of Theresa and doesn’t quite know what to do about it. <br><br>Okay, so the summary/blurb is okay right? I’ve read the summary so many times and every time I read it, I thought to myself, it’s just not my thing, BUT I kept on going back to the raving reviews and just decided to give it a go, if anything else, I could pick up another book.<br><br>Within the first page, you are hit <b>BAM</b> with jam pack drama and <b>I was tingling with excitement</b>. I was really shock with all the intensity, especially reading from the first chapter. I actually was so upset I started late at night knowing I couldn’t finish until the next day.<br><br><i>THE UNWANTED WIFE</i> was written in Theresa’s POV and she really is the <b>perfect Heroine</b>. I didn’t think Theresa was weak nor a doormat, I truly felt she just had enough. Realistically, I am not sure if any sane women could be in an emotional abusive relationship for a year and 8 months, but it’s a story and I went with it.<br><br><b>I LOVED LOVED LOVED Alessandro</b>, mind you I shook my head when I read his past mishaps, but really he’s my ideal Hero. He’s very angry, aggressive and wears his heart on his sleeve. Even though everything was from Theresa’s POV, I understood and saw Alessandro’s frustrations. I really enjoyed his character from page 1 to the ending.<br><br>There was a lot of character build up and I am so glad a lot of the questions were answered in the beginning of the story. The main story is simply about Alessandro and Theresa’s relationship. <b>I can’t tell you enough how much I enjoy these kinds of books.</b> <br> <br>Even though I wish it was longer and I wish I could read from Alessandro’s POV, there were so many things I look for in a book and got ten-folds in <i>THE UNWANTED WIFE</i>. I loved reading the story in chronological order (I can’t stand flash backs). I LOVED the HEAVY DRAMA and high tension, especially the back and forth banter. I loved the character development and having my ideal Hero and Heroine characters. <br><br>I truly believe the reviews would have given a 5 star rating if it wasn’t for the grammar mistakes, but this is a self published book, so it’s something I’m very okay with over-looking. I look at the writing style and plot, not necessarily if it’s grammatically correct. <br><br><i>THE UNWANTED WIFE</i> is a GREAT read and I recommend!!!<br><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16056862.The_Unwanted_Wife__Unwanted___1_" title="The Unwanted Wife (Unwanted, #1) by Natasha Anders" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1349084566s/16056862.jpg" alt="The Unwanted Wife (Unwanted, #1) by Natasha Anders" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><a href="http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/1477818065/ref=as_li_qf_sp_asin_tl?ie=UTF8&amp;camp=211189&amp;creative=373489&amp;creativeASIN=1477818065&amp;link_code=as3&amp;tag=jacqsread-20" rel="nofollow noopener">AMAZON</a><br><br>For more reviews, visit <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://jacquelinesreads.blogspot.com/">http://jacquelinesreads.blogspot.com/</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="14527664230094004713" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_530757099" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/530757099" />
    <a title="Didi" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6082482-didi"><img alt="Didi" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1459297426p2/6082482.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/530757099?book_show_action=true">Feb 08, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Didi" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Didi" href="/user/show/6082482-didi">Didi</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6082482-didi?shelf=enemies-to-lovers">enemies-to-lovers</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6082482-didi?shelf=angst-in-my-pants">angst-in-my-pants</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6082482-didi?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6082482-didi?shelf=betrayal">betrayal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6082482-didi?shelf=second-chances">second-chances</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer530757099" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16672441815470500072">Once I picked this up, I had a hard time putting it down. It was really good. My heart broke for Theresa and the veil of deceit she lived under. Her father was a bad and ruthless man putting his daughters happiness at stake and jeopardizing her life. While at first I didn't like Sandro at all, he was a genuine ass, he transformed into an incredible and dedicated man.<br/>It was his turnaround that impressed me. Believing Theresa well aware of her fathers trickery, he sought to make her life hell. No </span>
  <span id="freeText16672441815470500072" style="display:none">Once I picked this up, I had a hard time putting it down. It was really good. My heart broke for Theresa and the veil of deceit she lived under. Her father was a bad and ruthless man putting his daughters happiness at stake and jeopardizing her life. While at first I didn't like Sandro at all, he was a genuine ass, he transformed into an incredible and dedicated man.<br />It was his turnaround that impressed me. Believing Theresa well aware of her fathers trickery, he sought to make her life hell. No touching unless in the throes of sex, no kissing or any form of affection in any way, he made sure Theresa knew how little respect and love he had for her. <br /><br />But when he clued in, wow! He cleaned up in the most admirable of ways. My problem with this book lies with Theresa, however. I completely understood her suspicions when Sandro turned a new leaf. For almost 2 years, he had mistreated her, so being wary of him was expected. She wanted to leave him--legit, but what pissed me off was her insistence and stubbornness regarding Sandro's change of heart. Even when it became obvious to her friends and family that Sandro was genuine, she pushed and pushed. I wanted to slap her after a while! <br /><br />Regardless, Sandro and Theresa really persevered in the face of scrutiny and her fathers manipulation. Loved Sandro's vulnerability and Theresa's eventual ability to trust him again. The epilogue was sweet and nothing short of a lovely new beginning! Really looking forward to Bryce's story in, A Husband's Regret. </span>
  <a data-text-id="16672441815470500072" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('UdDkYgNZjfoeI4HgI7F5TJn0G3Ck3H2TuxtR9ZBa4wkWdietOueyXYZtZp+l3kavrZWtHDFViUCSOaVkL5N+7A==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('DxnzzPG6Yp3GQpIvZfMlC2/cTZMLzPpGseQCB//RHW5IvzADyARdOl4MdVDjnBroW737/55FDpWYxvaWQBiAiw==')})
  }

          <div class='bookAuthorProfile'>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__topContainer'>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__photoContainer'>
<a href="/author/show/6544265.Natasha_Anders"><div class='bookAuthorProfile__photo' style='background-image: url(https://images.gr-assets.com/authors/1592738312p3/6544265.jpg);'></div>

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer8811767496042248276">Since making her publishing debut in 2012, Natasha Anders has drawn praise and attention as a unique voice in romance. Montlake author and 2018 RITA® Finalist, Anders was born in Cape Town, South Africa. She spent nine years as an associate English teacher in Niigata, Japan, where she became a legendary karaoke diva. Anders currently lives in Cape Town.</span>

</div>
